## Testing resiliency using chaos engineering
**TAGS**: Architecture,Session
In this session, you learn how to use chaos engineering to set up failure injection testing to validate the resiliency of your service. Referencing the AWS Well-Architected Framework, you learn about the design principles and AWS resources that help ensure a resilient architecture. Then, with a three-tier architecture, this session demonstrates how to implement automation to simulate various failures, from the loss of a single Amazon EC2 server to the loss of an entire Availability Zone. The session focuses on the impacts of these failures and the resources that AWS provides to maintain high service availability and short time to recovery.

## Train large models with billions of parameters in TensorFlow 2.0 
**TAGS**: Artificial Intelligence & Machine Learning,Open Source,Enterprise/Migration,Architecture,Session
When training with large models or large inputs, a single GPU’s memory is often a limiting factor during training, producing out-of-memory (OOM) errors. The solution to this problem is model parallelism, which places layers or operations of a model on multiple GPU devices to utilize the aggregate memory of all GPUs in the cluster. But implementing model parallelism efficiently is hard, time-consuming, and requires expertise in graph partitioning and setting up execution pipelines. In this session, learn how to train large models with billions of parameters using Amazon SageMaker and TensorFlow 2.0.

## Turbocharge the AWS CDK with AWS Solutions Constructs
**TAGS**: DevOps,Session

## Turbocharging query execution on Amazon EMR
**TAGS**: Analytics,Session
Join this session to learn about the performance improvements made in Amazon EMR for Apache Spark and Presto, giving Amazon EMR one of the fastest runtimes for analytics workloads in the cloud. This session dives deep into how AWS generates smart query plans in the absence of accurate table statistics. It also covers adaptive query execution—a technique to dynamically collect statistics during query execution—and how AWS uses dynamic partition pruning to generate query predicates for speeding up table joins. You also learn about execution improvements such as data prefetching and pruning of nested data types.

## Unify access to siloed data with AWS AppSync GraphQL resolvers 
**TAGS**: Front-End Web & Mobile Development,Architecture,Business Apps (including Connect),Databases,Session

## Untangling multi-account management with ConsoleMe
**TAGS**: Netflix,DevOps,Session
At Netflix, the Cloud Infrastructure Security Team manages IAM permissions across hundreds of accounts, coordinating with users’ varied AWS experience. In this session, explore a Netflix tool, ConsoleMe, developed to address this issue securely, reduce inconsistencies and delays experienced by end users, and lower the multi-account management burden. ConsoleMe simplifies IAM permissions management by showing Netflix cloud resources in a single interface. It provides a multistep, dynamic, self-service wizard, which determines permissions, generates resource policies automatically, and uses Zelkova to intelligently apply low-risk permission requests. ConsoleMe also brokers application AWS credentials to provide users with short-lived IAM credentials for testing and development.

GitOps is being adopted by organizations that want to manage the ever-increasing complexity and sophistication of today’s workloads. With GitOps, they can increase the pace of innovation while maintaining enterprise-level security and compliance. In this session, learn how to use GitOps principles like version control, code review, and CI/CD to manage collaboration and compliance in almost any environment, from legacy systems to sophisticated cloud-native microservices. A session demo shows how to use infrastructure as code to manage containers on AWS. Learn how the principles can be applied to any service from AWS Fargate, Amazon ECS, and Amazon EKS to Amazon EC2, AWS Lambda, and VMware on AWS. This presentation is brought to you by GitLab, an AWS Partner.

## Usando Machine Learning para combater evasão escolar
**TAGS**: Portuguese,Artificial Intelligence & Machine Learning,Analytics,Public Sector,Serverless,Session
A Betha Sistemas é uma parceira AWS que desenvolve soluções para mais de 800 prefeituras no Brasil. Em 2019 ela começou a oferecer às secretarias municipais de educação de 20 municípios a capacidade de usar o aprendizado de maquina (ML) para prever evasão e reprovação escolar dos alunos do ensino fundamental. Nesta sessão, iremos mostrar como essa solução foi construída utilizando dados escolares históricos, para alimentar um algoritmo de previsão hospedado no Amazon Sagemaker. Ajudando na tomada de decisões proativamente. Finalmente, mostraremos os resultados obtidos e como essa solução pode ser expandida.

## Use AWS Firewall Manager to audit overpermissive security groups

## Use Amazon GuardDuty and AWS Security Hub to secure multiple accounts
**TAGS**: Session
This session provides you with account-level considerations, best practices, and guidance to help structure and manage security across multiple AWS accounts and on-premises operations. It covers the benefits of aggregating, parsing, and remediating security findings at scale using services such as Amazon GuardDuty and AWS Security Hub, and it reviews integrations with external SIEM systems. GuardDuty and Security Hub help filter findings to reduce noise prior to ingesting data into a SIEM. Come learn how to coordinate these services across accounts for a single source of truth for security findings.

## Use data to optimize your daily fantasy sports football lineups

## Using AI to automatically find insights in email: A rapid prototyping story

## Using AWS Transit Gateway for your multicast workloads
**TAGS**: Networking & Content Delivery,Session
Multicast routing quickly distributes copies of the same data from one source to multiple receivers. This is a common design for media distribution (video conferencing, for example) or for when end destinations get the same information quickly and at roughly the same time (such as a stock ticker). AWS Transit Gateway routes multicast traffic between subnets of attached VPCs and serves as a multicast router for instances, sending traffic destined for multiple receiving instances. This session covers recent AWS Transit Gateway multicast updates and includes a quick demo of passing a message from a sender to multiple subscribers.

## Using AWS WAF and AWS Secrets Manager to enforce Amazon CloudFront origins
**TAGS**: Session
When delivering web applications through Amazon CloudFront, a common objective is to prevent viewer requests from directly accessing origin resources. Preventing viewer requests from bypassing CloudFront helps ensure all traffic is handled by global edge locations and is processed according to your AWS WAF rule set prior to being forwarded to your origin endpoint. This session covers common origin enforcement approaches with a deeper focus on how to use CloudFront, AWS WAF, and AWS Secrets Manager to prevent viewer requests from directly accessing your origin resources.

**TAGS**: Databases,Session
Data integrity is an important feature of business applications built on databases, and auditing is a required element in database system-of-record design. In this session, learn how early Amazon QLDB users are applying the ledger database’s unique properties for data provenance and cryptographic verifiability to implement systems of record with data integrity built-in rather than added as a secondary consideration.

## 华米基于AWS构建全球云上健康服务
**TAGS**: Chinese,Architecture,Databases,Compute,Healthcare,Session
华米科技是全球TOP5的智能可穿戴设备制造商，在全球拥有近1亿用户，如何为用户提供安全，稳定，高效的服务，是华米技术团队一直在思考的问题，利用AWS全球资源的能力，以及云原生的架构，在统一技术栈的前提下，华米基于ECS,DynamoDB,Aurora,WAF等产品实现了高效部署安全,稳定的云上健康服务的目标。随着国内迁移的结束，All-in AWS更是华米对AWS的信任。

## 在云端运行你的Tiny ML 推理
**TAGS**: Chinese,Artificial Intelligence & Machine Learning,Serverless,Session
TinyML 是一个快速增长的机器学习技术和应用的方向。通常我们是在边缘侧或者低功耗的微处理器实现这一类机器学习的推理，并由此而产生了一系列与此相对应的工具与技术，例如Tensorflow Lite、OpenVino 、OpenCV以及Darknet 等。在这个演讲中，我们讲探讨如何利用这些高效推理的技术，利用AWS Lambda 作为推理的平台而将TinyML 运行在云端。这种实现的方式对于需要简单部署、高效推理的场景来说尤为有效。

## 基于SageMaker构建海外智能推荐平台
**TAGS**: Chinese,Artificial Intelligence & Machine Learning,Consumer/Packaged Goods,Session
如何快速的构建、训练和部署机器学习模型不仅是业务部门关注的重点，更是研发部门渴求的目标。通过使用Amazon SageMaker，OPPO在海外智能推荐和机器学习的业务场景中，完美的消除了各个过程中繁重的重复工作，让开发、训练、构建和部署高质量的模型变得更加的轻松和灵活。OPPO将分享在海外使用Amazon SageMaker优化智能推荐平台和模型的最佳实践经验。

## 文远知行Robotaxi开放运营背后的数据力量
**TAGS**: Chinese,Automotive,Artificial Intelligence & Machine Learning,IoT,Session
文远知行是一家拥有中国领先L4级自动驾驶技术的智能出行公司，是中国首家得到全球汽车制造商投资的L4级自动驾驶初创企业，也是中国第一家获准开展全无人驾驶路测的自动驾驶公司。截至2020年9月底，文远知行无人驾驶车队规模超100辆，自动驾驶总里程超过300万公里，Robotaxi全对外开放运营超过300天，接待乘客超过100,000人次，无任何主动责任事故。本次演讲介绍文远知行如何利用AWS构建自动驾驶整体方案并利用PB级数据支撑技术创新。

## 汇量科技基于 AWS 构建日均千亿次预测的一站式机器学习平台
**TAGS**: Chinese,Artificial Intelligence & Machine Learning,Analytics,Advertising & Marketing,Session
Mobvisa汇量科技是全球领先的移动营销平台，每天需要通过复杂的算法预测获得超过1000亿个广告请求，这一需求的背后，是每天数十个PB的数据处理规模、每小时数十亿个特征规模的模型训练，以及每天数万次的分析和模型训练工作。这对解决方案的高存储吞吐量与弹性要求，达到近乎严苛的地步。如何满足高吞吐量、高弹性的同时，实现成本上的优化与节省，是面临的首要挑战。

## 番組完成素材を一元的に管理するコンテンツ管理システムの構築
**TAGS**: Japanese,Session
フジテレビでは、将来の新たな視聴サービスや増加し続けるコンテンツ送出先に柔軟に対応するため、従来のやり方から脱却し、最適化された放送設備・ワークフローの構築に取り組んできました。 S3とS3 Glacier、MediaConvertを活用した「総合コンテンツ管理システム」は、社内設備を最小限にしたシンプルな構成です。番組素材を一元的に管理する新しい「コンテンツレイク」として、放送用番組素材だけではなくインターネット動画配信や外部販売用の番組素材を扱うほか、アーカイブシステムも包括しています。

## 고객 비즈니스 성공을 위한 AWS 인공 지능 서비스 소개
**TAGS**: Korean,Artificial Intelligence & Machine Learning,Innovation,Session
인공 지능과 기계 학습 (AI/ML)은 기업의 차별화를 만듭니다. AWS는 고객의 비즈니스의 다양한 측면에서 클라우드를 기반으로 새로운 AI/ML 기능을 구축 할 수 있도록 지원하고 있습니다. AWS를 이용하면 여러분은 기계 학습을 통해 데이터에서 더 쉽게 통찰력을 얻을 수 있습니다. 현재 AWS ML 서비스는 고객의 성공을 위해 계속 성장하고 있습니다. 이 세션에서는 다양한 AWS 최신 기계 학습 서비스, 고객의 가치를 위한 ML 서비스 개발 및 고객의 주요 모범 사례를 통해 지능형 비즈니스에 AWS를 채택한 방법을 소개합니다.

## 대용량 자바 애플리케이션 클라우드 네이티브 아키텍처 적용기
**TAGS**: Korean,DevOps,Architecture,Containers,Enterprise/Migration,Session
Samsung Account는 10억 개 이상의 계정과 2억 명의 활성 사용자를 가지고 있으며, 2018년에 주요 서비스 중단을 경험한 이후 클라우드 네이티브 엔터프라이즈 자바 애플리케이션으로 마이그레이션했습니다. 이 세션에서는 엔터프라이즈 자바 애플리케이션을 클라우드 네이티브 아키텍처로 변경하는 동안 테스트 하고 공부했던 다양한 경험들을 4가지의 단계로 나눠서 1)도커라이징 2) DevOps 오케스트레이션 3) 네트워크, 로드 밸런싱 4) 카오스 엔지니어링 항목으로 설명합니다.

## 서버리스 기반 인공 지능 서비스를 이용한 무인 스마트 매장 구현하기
**TAGS**: Korean,Retail,Artificial Intelligence & Machine Learning,Serverless,Session
현대백화점그룹은 고품격 백화점부터 아울렛 그리고 면세점까지 다양한 오프라인 리테일 채널을 통해 쇼핑 문화를 선도하고 있습니다. 향후 미래형 무인 스마트 매장을 오픈하여 고객들에게 새로운 쇼핑 경험을 제공할 예정입니다. 이 세션에서는 AWS 프로토타이핑팀과 함께 AWS의 인공지능 서비스와 서버리스 서비스들을 활용하여 빠르고 효과적으로 무인 스마트 매장을 구현한 사례를 소개합니다.

## 시계열 분석을 사용한 수요 예측 및 재고 관리 최적화 사례
**TAGS**: Korean,Retail,Artificial Intelligence & Machine Learning,Enterprise/Migration,Session
소매업을 포함한 많은 기업들은 기계 학습을 디지털 혁신을 위한 핵심 기술로 사용하는 것을 고려하고 있습니다. 이 세션에서는 소매 비즈니스 최적화를위한 수요 예측 및 재고 관리에 대한 시계열 분석에 Amazon Forecast 및 Amazon SageMaker를 사용하는 방법을 공유합니다. 이를 기반으로 국내 대형 유통 업체가 재고 서비스를 최적화 한 성공 사례를 공유합니다.

## 우아한형제들의 클라우드 여정
**TAGS**: Korean,Startup,Front-End Web & Mobile Development,Travel & Hospitality,Financial Services,Session
우아한형제들은 월 천만명 이상의 활성 사용자를 보유한 국내 음식 배달 서비스의 선두 주자입니다. 2016년 AWS 클라우드 이전을 결정한 이후, 비즈니스 확장에 맞게 모든 워크로드를 AWS로 이전해왔습니다. 이 세션에서는 그동안 경험한 클라우드로의 마이그레이션에 대한 과제와 모범 사례를 공유합니다.
